Lowe FarmLowe Farm School (23-1st St. E. Lowe Farm)December 1 2 and 3 2020 A confirmed case of COVID-19 was in the school on Dec. 1 2 and 3. Based on the public health investigation this exposure was assessed to be low risk overall for the school community. Classroom contacts are being advised to monitor for symptoms and seek testing if symptoms develop. Close contacts connected to the case have been identified and advised to self-isolate. Anyone who is a close contact has been contacted via an email from public health. The school will remain open to all other students and staff who can continue to attend school in person.
